<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">ITEM&#160;2.02</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">RESULTS OF OPERATIONS AND FINANCIAL CONDITION </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On December&#160;21, 2021, Apogee Enterprises, Inc. issued a press release announcing its financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2022. A copy of this press release is furnished (not filed) as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g231221dsp01.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Press Release </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR
RELEASE:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;December&nbsp;21, 2021 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>APOGEE ENTERPRISES REPORTS FISCAL 2022 THIRD QUARTER RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&#149;</I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Third-quarter revenue grows 6.6&nbsp;percent, to $334&nbsp;million </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&#149;</I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Third-quarter earnings of $0.44 per diluted share, which includes $6.4&nbsp;million of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> restructuring and impairment costs </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&#149;</I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Adjusted earnings of $0.63 per diluted share </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&#149;</I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Continued strong cash flow, with $86&nbsp;million of cash from operations year to date
</I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>MINNEAPOLIS, MN, December</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;21, 2021 &#150; Apogee Enterprises, Inc. (Nasdaq: APOG)</B> today announced its
fiscal 2022 third-quarter results. Third-quarter revenue grew 6.6&nbsp;percent to $334.2&nbsp;million, compared to $313.6&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal year 2021, led by growth in Architectural Services and Architectural Framing
Systems. Third quarter earnings were $0.44 per diluted share, which included $3.4&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> costs related to previously announced restructuring actions and $3.0&nbsp;million of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> costs for the impairment of a minority equity investment. This compares to earnings of $1.42 per diluted share in last year&#146;s third quarter, which included a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $19.3&nbsp;million on the sale of a building and $1.4&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> costs related to COVID. Adjusted earnings in the third quarter were $0.63
per diluted share, compared to $0.90 in the third quarter of fiscal 2021.<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1 </SUP> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Commentary </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;As we outlined in our recent investor day, we are shifting Apogee&#146;s focus to become the economic leader in our target markets, while building the
operating model and capabilities needed to enable profitable growth,&#148; said Ty R. Silberhorn, Chief Executive Officer. &#147;During the third quarter, we drove further progress on our new strategic plan. We continued to execute the restructuring
and cost reduction actions we announced in August, made progress implementing our enterprise transformation initiatives, and relaunched our Lean and continuous improvement program. In the coming quarters, we expect to continue our strategic pivot,
positioning Apogee for improved operating performance.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjusted earnings and adjusted earnings per share are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial measures. See Use and Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures later in this press release for more information and a reconciliation to the most directly comparable GAAP measures.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Apogee Enterprises,
Inc.</B> &#149; 4400 West 78<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> Street &#149; Minneapolis, MN 55435 &#149; (952) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">835-1874</FONT> &#149; www.apog.com </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Apogee Enterprises, Inc. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
 2
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mr.&nbsp;Silberhorn continued, &#147;While we are still early into our transformation journey, these efforts
are beginning to be reflected in our financial results. Earnings this quarter improved sequentially compared to the second quarter, with encouraging progress on both revenue growth and margin expansion. We also continued to generate strong cash
flow, further improving the company&#146;s financial position. I am proud of our team for delivering these results despite continued cost inflation and supply chain challenges.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Segment Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Architectural Framing Systems
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Architectural Framing Systems revenue grew 11&nbsp;percent, to $151.7&nbsp;million, from $136.7&nbsp;million in the prior-year period, primarily
driven by flow-through from pricing actions taken to offset inflation. Third-quarter operating income increased to $10.7&nbsp;million, up from $7.2&nbsp;million in last year&#146;s third quarter, primarily driven by improved pricing and the benefits
from restructuring actions, which offset the impact of cost inflation. Segment backlog increased to $419&nbsp;million, compared to $406&nbsp;million at the end of the second quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Architectural Glass </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Architectural Glass revenue in the
third quarter was $74.3&nbsp;million, compared to $84.8&nbsp;million in the prior-year quarter, primarily reflecting lower volume, partially offset by an improved sales mix. Architectural Glass had a third-quarter operating loss of $(1.3) million,
which included $3.5&nbsp;million of restructuring costs. Excluding these costs, third-quarter adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $2.2&nbsp;million, compared to $10.8&nbsp;million in last year&#146;s
third quarter. Architectural Glass&#146; results in last year&#146;s third quarter included $7.4&nbsp;million of operating income related to a New Markets Tax Credit transaction. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Architectural Services </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Architectural Services revenue
grew 20&nbsp;percent to $92.0&nbsp;million, up from $76.7&nbsp;million in the prior-year quarter, driven by increased volume from executing projects in backlog. Third-quarter operating income increased to $9.2&nbsp;million, compared to
$8.6&nbsp;million in the prior-year period, primarily reflecting the increased volume, partially offset by a less favorable project mix. Segment backlog of $572&nbsp;million was unchanged from the end of the second quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Large-Scale Optical </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Large-Scale Optical revenue grew
8&nbsp;percent to $27.4&nbsp;million, up from $25.3&nbsp;million in the third quarter last year, primarily driven by a more favorable sales mix. Operating income was $6.0&nbsp;million, compared to $26.1&nbsp;million in last year&#146;s third
quarter. Last year&#146;s third quarter included a $19.3&nbsp;million gain on the sale of a building. Third-quarter adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $6.0&nbsp;million, compared to $6.8&nbsp;million
in the prior-year period, primarily reflecting short-term costs for expedited freight, partially offset by the more favorable sales mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate and
Other </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Corporate and other costs in the third quarter increased to $6.9&nbsp;million, up from $3.0&nbsp;million in the prior-year quarter, primarily
due to increased health care costs. Corporate and other costs in last year&#146;s third quarter included $1.4&nbsp;million of COVID-related costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Condition </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal year to date, net cash
provided by operating activities was $86.3&nbsp;million, compared to $120.5&nbsp;million in the first nine months of fiscal 2021. Cash flow in the prior-year period benefited from reduced working capital and temporary actions related to COVID.
Capital expenditures through the first nine months of the fiscal year were $13.1&nbsp;million, down from $17.1&nbsp;million in the same period last year, as the company slowed some investments while it conducted its strategic review. In the third
quarter, the company repurchased 165,851 shares of stock for $6.7&nbsp;million. Fiscal year to date, the company has returned $44.2&nbsp;million of cash to shareholders through share repurchases and dividend payments, up from $35.3&nbsp;million in
the first nine months of fiscal 2021. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjusted operating income is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. See Use and
Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures later in this press release for more information and a reconciliation to the most directly comparable GAAP measures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Apogee Enterprises,
Inc.</B> &#149; 4400 West 78<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> Street &#149; Minneapolis, MN 55435 &#149; (952) 835-1874 &#149; www.apog.com </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Apogee Enterprises, Inc. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
 3
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Quarter-end</FONT> total debt was $163&nbsp;million, compared to
$168&nbsp;million at the end of last year&#146;s third quarter. Cash and cash equivalents were $78.3&nbsp;million, compared to $55.4&nbsp;million at the end of the third quarter of fiscal 2021.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Restructuring </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On August&nbsp;11, 2021, the company
announced plans to realign and simplify its business structure. During the third quarter, the company incurred an additional $3.4&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> restructuring charges related to this announcement,
bringing the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-date</FONT></FONT> total to $24.2&nbsp;million. In the third quarter, $3.6&nbsp;million of restructuring costs were included in cost of sales and $(0.2) million
were included in selling, general and administrative expenses, for the reversal of previously accrued severance. The company anticipates $2&nbsp;million to $3&nbsp;million of additional <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> restructuring
costs in the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company is narrowing its guidance for full-year adjusted earnings to a range of $2.25 to $2.40 per diluted share, from the previous range of $2.20 to
$2.40. This guidance excludes the impact of restructuring and impairment costs. The company expects to record a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of approximately $19&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter, related to the previously
announced sale of its Architectural Glass facility in Statesboro, Georgia. The company intends to exclude this gain from its adjusted earnings results. The company continues to expect a long-term average tax rate of approximately 24.5&nbsp;percent
and now expects full-year capital expenditures of approximately $25&nbsp;million, down from the previous estimate of approximately $35&nbsp;million, as the company has slowed some investments while it conducted its strategic review. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call Information </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company will host a
conference call today at 8:00 a.m. Central Time to discuss its financial results and provide a business update. This call will be webcast and is available in the Investor Relations section of the company&#146;s website, along with presentation
slides, at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.apog.com/events-and-presentations</FONT></FONT></U>. The webcast also will be archived for replay on the company&#146;s website. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Apogee Enterprises </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Apogee Enterprises, Inc.
(Nasdaq: APOG) delivers distinctive solutions for enclosing commercial buildings and framing art. Headquartered in Minneapolis, MN, we are a leader in architectural products and services, providing architectural glass, aluminum framing systems and
installation services for buildings, as well as value-added glass and acrylic for custom picture framing and displays. For more information, visit <U>www.apog.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This release and other financial communications may contain the following <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adjusted operating income, adjusted operating margin, adjusted net earnings and adjusted earnings per diluted
share (&#147;adjusted earnings per share&#148; or &#147;adjusted EPS&#148;) are used by the company to provide meaningful supplemental information about its operating performance by excluding amounts that are not considered part of core operating
results to enhance comparability of results from period to period. Examples of items excluded to arrive at this adjusted measure in recent reporting periods include: impairment charges, restructuring costs, acquired project-related charges, proceeds
from significant asset sales, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related expenditures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Apogee Enterprises,
Inc.</B> &#149; 4400 West 78<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> Street &#149; Minneapolis, MN 55435 &#149; (952) 835-1874 &#149; www.apog.com </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Apogee Enterprises, Inc. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
 4
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities, minus capital expenditures. The company
considers this measure an indication of its financial strength. However, free cash flow does not fully reflect the company&#146;s ability to freely deploy generated cash, as it does not reflect, for example, required payments on indebtedness and
other fixed obligations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net Debt is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure defined as the sum of long-term and
current debt on our consolidated balance sheet, less cash and cash equivalents. The company considers this measure helpful to evaluate our capital structure and financial leverage, and our ability to fund investing and financing activities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adjusted EBITDA represents net income before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization and certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> and other adjustment items. We believe this metric provides useful information to investors and analysts about the Company&#146;s performance because
it eliminates the effects of certain items that are unusual in nature or whose fluctuation from period to period do not necessarily correspond to changes in the operations of the company. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Another <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operational measure that management uses is backlog. Backlog represents the dollar amount of signed
contracts or firm orders, generally as a result of a competitive bidding process, which is expected to be recognized as revenue. Backlog is not a term defined under U.S. GAAP and is not a measure of contract profitability. Backlog should not be used
as the sole indicator of future segment revenue because we have a substantial number of projects with short lead times that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">book-and-bill</FONT></FONT> within the same reporting
period and are not included in backlog. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures to evaluate the company&#146;s
historical and prospective financial performance, measure operational profitability on a consistent basis, and provide enhanced transparency to the investment community. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be
viewed in addition to, and not as a substitute for, the reported financial results of the company prepared in accordance with GAAP. Other companies may calculate these measures differently, limiting the usefulness of the measures for comparison with
other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic; (B)&nbsp;global economic conditions and the cyclical nature of the North American and Latin American commercial construction industries, which impact our three architectural segments, and
consumer confidence and the condition of the U.S. economy, which impact our large-scale optical segment; (C)&nbsp;fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates; (D)&nbsp;actions of new and existing competitors; (E)&nbsp;ability to effectively
utilize and increase production capacity; (F)&nbsp;departure of key personnel and ability to source sufficient labor; (G)&nbsp;product performance, reliability and quality issues; (H)&nbsp;project management and installation issues that could affect

<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustment related to previously announced decision to exit certain operations in the Architectural Glass
segment and reorganize operations within the Architectural Framing Systems segment, including $1.3&nbsp;million of asset impairment charges, $1.4&nbsp;million of employee termination costs and $0.7&nbsp;million of other costs associated with these
restructuring plans incurred during the third quarter of fiscal 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustment for impairment of minority equity investment is a result of the assignment for the benefit of
creditors of all of the assets of a company in which Apogee holds a minority interest. The impairment represents a write-down of Apogee&#146;s entire investment in the company. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Gain on sale of building within the Large-Scale Optical segment during the third quarter of fiscal 2021.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustment for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19-related</FONT></FONT>
costs, primarily incremental labor costs due to quarantine-related absenteeism and personal protective equipment for employees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
